  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_057b6156-b0d5-4c56-bc48-2262a2f8793c'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer6866372428525335409">Death Note, Vol. 6: Give-and-Take (Death Note #6), Tsugumi Ohba, Takeshi Obata (Illustrator), Alexis Kirsch (Translator)<br/><br/>تهران : جنگل‏‫، 1398‬‏‫= 2020 م‬<br/><br/>Although they've collected plenty of evidence tying the seven Yotsuba members to the newest Kira, Light, L and the rest of the task force are no closer to discovering which one actually possesses the Death Note.   <span id="freeText6866372428525335409" style="display:none">Death Note, Vol. 6: Give-and-Take (Death Note #6), Tsugumi Ohba, Takeshi Obata (Illustrator), Alexis Kirsch (Translator)<br /><br />تهران : جنگل‏‫، 1398‬‏‫= 2020 م‬<br /><br />Although they've collected plenty of evidence tying the seven Yotsuba members to the newest Kira, Light, L and the rest of the task force are no closer to discovering which one actually possesses the Death Note. Desperate for some headway, L recruits Misa to infiltrate the group and feed them information calculated to bring Kira into the open. But the Shinigami Rem reveals to Misa who the Kiras really are, and, armed with this knowledge, Misa will do anything to help Light.<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز<br /><br />عنوان: دفتر مرگ: کتاب شش بده بستان؛ نویسنده: تسوگومی اوبا؛<br /><br />دفتر مرگ؛ نام یک مجموعه مانگای ژاپنی است از تسوگومی اوبا (نویسنده) و تاکه‌شی اوباتا (طراح) که از روی آن یک مجموعه تلویزیونی انیمه هم ساخته شده است. دفتر مرگ برای نخستین بار از ماه دسامبر سال 2003 میلادی تا ماه می سال 2006 میلادی در مجله هفته‌ نامه شونن جامپ انتشارات شوئیشا به چاپ می‌رسید. «لایت یاگامی»، مرد جوانی است که از جرم و بزهکاری بیزار است، تصادفاً دفتری پیدا می‌کند که رویش نوشته‌ شده (دفتر مرگ). در صفحه ی نخست دفتر توضیح داده شده که اگر نام شخصی در دفتر نوشته شود و نویسنده در همان حال چهره ی شخص را در ذهنش مجسم کند، آن شخص پس ازچهل ثانیه بر اثر حمله قلبی خواهد مرد. «لایت» در صدد استفاده از دفتر برمی‌آید. و ...؛<br /><br />یاگامی لایت (کیرا)؛ لایت؛ شخصیت اصلی دفتر مرگ، یک پسر بسیار باهوشی است که در حدود هفده سال سن دارد. هنگامی که دفتر مرگ توسط ریوک (یکی از خدایان مرگ)، در دنیای انسان‌ها انداخته شد، لایت نخستین کسی بود که به طور اتفاقی با این دفترچه روبرو شده و پی به راز آن می‌بَرَد و خلافکارها را می‌کشد. در این حال مردمان به او لقب کیرا (قاتل) می‌دهند، در این حال لایت (کیرا) برای پاک کردن پلیدی از دنیا و ساختن آرمانشهر و حکم‌رانی بر دنیای جدید، دست به کشتن انسان‌های فاسد می‌زند و او خودش را عدالت خطاب می‌کند. «لایت» که می‌دانست «ال» کارگاه زبردستی است برای اینکه بتواند او را از معرکه خارج کند توسط پدرش که سمت رئیس پلیسی ژاپن را بر عهده دارد به «ال» می‌پیوندد و به او در پیدا کردن و دستگیری «کیرا» کمک می‌کند، اما سرانجام لایت با نقشه‌ ای از پیش تعریف شده توانست «ال» را به قتل برساند غافل از اینکه شخصیت دیگری در داستان وجود دارد، که به بعد از مرگ «ال»، با عنوان «ان (نیئر)» در ادامه داستان رونمایی می‌شود و ادامه کار «ال» را به عهده می‌گیرد و...؛ <br /><br />ا. شربیانی</span>

  <span id="freeText13330426251908115618" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers</b><br /><br />-Didn't find the Yotsuba arc all that engrossing, the characters were boring and too numerous, and their motivations were uninspired and cliched.<br /><br />-The investigation L and Light were carrying out was also a little dull and rather repetitive, the investigation was only properly entertaining when Misa was involved.<br /><br />-L kind of annoyed me in this one, I got tired of him over analysing everything. He irritated me so much that I was actually rooting for Light to outsmart him and get away with everything. Both characters weren't as interesting as they used to be.<br /><br />-Misa was still the best character. I loved how much Rem cared for her and looked out for her, it was really sweet.<br /><br />-I was glad Matsuda lived, he reminded me of a male Misa, he was so funny and cute.<br /><br />-Really loved the ending with the chase for Higuchi/other Kira. <br /></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6881350725810246165">The investigations about the new Kira continue, with many twists and a pace that becomes faster. There are less mental games between Light and 'L', thing that appeared a bit too heavy in the recent volumes and I think this book will mark another turning point in the story. There is more space reserved for investigations about Kira and Yotsuba members.<br/><br/>The final part it’s particularly exciting and you can read it in a single breath, with a pace that keep the reader glued up, until an incredible en</span>
  <span id="freeText6881350725810246165" style="display:none">The investigations about the new Kira continue, with many twists and a pace that becomes faster. There are less mental games between Light and 'L', thing that appeared a bit too heavy in the recent volumes and I think this book will mark another turning point in the story. There is more space reserved for investigations about Kira and Yotsuba members.<br /><br />The final part it’s particularly exciting and you can read it in a single breath, with a pace that keep the reader glued up, until an incredible ending complete with a car chase, in a perfect action movies style.<br /><br />Another excellent chapter of this series. I must say that the idea of a new Kira, doesn’t convince me at first, for fear of get away from the original idea, but I think it was managed best.<br /><br />I cannot wait to read the next volume<br /></span>

<div id="review_1396914720" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1396914720" />
    <a title="Chayse Sundt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5365164-chayse-sundt"><img alt="Chayse Sundt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312379566p2/5365164.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1396914720?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chayse Sundt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chayse Sundt" href="/user/show/5365164-chayse-sundt">Chayse Sundt</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1396914720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10923280304748528028">Death Note is something I started because I was recommended it by someone who I value their opinion. But my expectations for this series has not been turning out to what my reaction is while reading it. And don’t take -that as a bad idea, because the series is so much more than I had hoped for.<br/><br/>This series has taken me on a whirlwind of adventure with different characters who all bring something new to every volume. Like mentioned in an earlier review, I felt that the manga might end soon but the</span>
  <span id="freeText10923280304748528028" style="display:none">Death Note is something I started because I was recommended it by someone who I value their opinion. But my expectations for this series has not been turning out to what my reaction is while reading it. And don’t take -that as a bad idea, because the series is so much more than I had hoped for.<br /><br />This series has taken me on a whirlwind of adventure with different characters who all bring something new to every volume. Like mentioned in an earlier review, I felt that the manga might end soon but there is always something waiting to keep me in its grasp and holding on.<br /><br />Light and L are still working together and now they are trying to unveil the new Kira that has appeared inside this business whose main goal is to take out their competitors and rise to the top. However the idea of risking lives is not becoming something Light, L, and the other members of their group to discuss and see if risking the lives of a couple individuals is okay if it means ending the reign of a compulsive killer.<br />There are so many twists and turns in this series that whenever you think something is going to happen something out of the blue pops out and it seems to be that the people in the book who start to have control of the Death Note are becoming more and more sinister. It just blows my mind to think of the power these people have and what they do it.<br /><br />Overall this is a manga that I recommend you check out and see where it will take you. I am highly enjoying it and will see it till the end.<br /><br />Happy Reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10923280304748528028" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText12150034319528903651" style="display:none">Summary of Vol. 1;<br /><br /><b>“The name of the human who is written in this note shall die.”</b><br /><br /><br /><br />Light Yagami is an ace student with great prospects - and he's bored out of his mind. But all that changes when he finds the Death Note, a notebook dropped by a rogue Shinigami, a death god. Any human whose name is written in the notebook dies, and now Light has vowed to use the power of the Death Note to rid the world of evil. But when criminals begin dropping dead, the authorities send the legendary detective L to track down the killer. With L hot on his heels, will Light lose sight of his noble goal...or his life?<br /><br />Boredom<br />Light tests the boundaries of the Death Note's powers as L and the police begin to close in. Luckily Light's father is the head of the Japanese National Police Agency and leaves vital information about the case lying around the house. With access to his father's files, Light can keep one step ahead of the authorities. But who is the strange man following him, and how can Light guard against enemies whose names he doesn't know?<br /><br />As you can expect by my rating this was fantastic! I can't say much about this particular volume as it is the 6th, but I would highly recommend the manga &amp; anime of this series.</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2243327092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12727666063935322780">I'm in the process of reading the entire Death Note series...rereading first several volumes (which I had read a few years ago), and then picking up with those volumes I hadn't read. This volume, and parts of the previous, has the storyline taking a less engaging turn, I feel. Nonetheless, by the end of this current volume, there's the promise of yet another turn...one that I find interesting. I'm not sure that Light/Kira and L working together was the most enjoyable part of the series so far.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6zMCZ/GYw0RKRNE/UZpEvMNiXSqsjWY5VznjdKZGwc9cZPj+LvWX7GzRsdf8LCOXf9U2ngBjMJTwDh094MjAKA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S5DYSdPr+bl1QdzUVwtiiwgYeT2OGvI66LdKtrNKqGX8xyLQDIatEVPUvDz6vQWgtK8SiSL0pJdPgLT/9cSpgg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1049942397775261319">Tsugumi Ōba (Profile in Japanese: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/19876928.______' title='大場 つぐみ' rel='nofollow noopener'>大場 つぐみ</a>), born in Tokyo, Japan, is a writer best known for the manga Death Note. His/her real identity is a closely guarded secret. As stated by the profile placed at the beginning of each Death Note manga, Ōba collects teacups and develops manga plots while holding his knees on a chair, similar to a habit of L, one of the main characters of the series.<br/><br/>There is spe</span>
  <span id="freeText1049942397775261319" style="display:none">Tsugumi Ōba (Profile in Japanese: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/19876928.______" title="大場 つぐみ" rel="nofollow noopener">大場 つぐみ</a>), born in Tokyo, Japan, is a writer best known for the manga Death Note. His/her real identity is a closely guarded secret. As stated by the profile placed at the beginning of each Death Note manga, Ōba collects teacups and develops manga plots while holding his knees on a chair, similar to a habit of L, one of the main characters of the series.<br /><br />There is speculation that Tsugumi Ōba is a pen name and that he is really Hiroshi Gamō. Pointing out that in Bakuman the main character's uncle was a one-hit wonder manga artist who worked on a gag super hero manga, very similar to Gamō and Tottemo! Luckyman in all aspects. Also that the storyboards drawn by Ōba greatly resemble Tottemo! Luckyman in style.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1049942397775261319" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
